                                  SalesLineLoc.SETRANGE("Document Type","Sales Line"."Document Type");
                                  SalesLineLoc.SETRANGE("Document No.","Sales Line"."Document No.");
                                  IF SalesLineLoc.FINDSET THEN
                                    REPEAT
                                      A := SalesLineLoc."Line Amount";
                                      IF (SalesLineLoc."VAT %" = 100) THEN BEGIN
                                      SalesLineLoc."Tax Amount (VAT)":=0;
                                      B := SalesLineLoc."Tax Amount (VAT)";
                                      END
                                      ELSE
                                      B:=SalesLineLoc."Tax Amount (VAT)";

                                      VarSlipAmount := VarSlipAmount+A+B;
                                    UNTIL SalesLineLoc.NEXT = 0;

                                  IF ("Sales Header"."Currency Code"<>'') THEN
                                  VarSlipAmountLCY:=VarSlipAmountLCY+Tot_WHT_LCY + Tot_Cust_LCY + Tot_Exchng_LCy_Dr_1+Tot_Exchng_LCy_Dr  //YIMMDEVIP1.0
                                  ELSE
                                  //VarSlipAmountLCY:=VarSlipAmountLCY+"Sales Line"."Line Amount"+"Sales Line"."Tax Amount (VAT)";  //YIMMDEVIP1.0
                                  VarSlipAmountLCY:= VarSlipAmount;
                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.end

                                  "Sales Header".MODIFY;




                                  //======================================SH Footer 5
                                  {
                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.begin
                                  User1.RESET;
                                  User1.SETRANGE("User Name",'%1',"Sales Header".UID);
                                  IF User1.FINDFIRST THEN
                                   Uname1:=User1."Full Name";


                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.end
                                  }

                                  IF (COMPANYNAME = MasterSetup1."Company Name TBI") THEN
                                     Section20:=FALSE;

                                  {
                                  IF (COMPANYNAME = MasterSetup1."Company Name YEID") THEN
                                    TextForSignature:='Purchase / Marketing'
                                  ELSE
                                  } //Commented as YEID does not exist currently.
                                   TextForSignature:='Purchase';

                                  //section sales header footer(5)/section 20--end

                                  //section sales header footer(6)/section 21--start

                                  IF (COMPANYNAME <> MasterSetup1."Company Name TBI") THEN
                                     Section21:=FALSE;



                                  //MESSAGE('dddd   '   +FORMAT(Section8));

                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
